    }
    
    if (empty($message)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°";
    }
    
    // ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î
    if (empty($errors)) {
        // ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á DB, ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•, etc.)
        echo "‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à";
    } else {
        // ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î
        foreach ($errors as $error) {
            echo "<p style='color: red;'>$error</p>";
        }
    }

<!-- HTML + JavaScript -->
<form id="contactForm">
    <input name="name" required placeholder="‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠">
    <input name="email" type="email" required placeholder="‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•">
    <button>‡∏™‡πà‡∏á</button>
</form>
<div id="result"></div>

<script>
document.getElementById("contactForm").addEventListener("submit", async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    
    const form = new FormData(e.target);
    
    try {
        const response = await fetch("/contact.php", {
            method: "POST",
            body: form
        });
        
        const text = await response.text();
        document.getElementById("result").textContent = text;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error:", error);
    }
});
</script>

    "message" => "‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì $name ($email)"

MySQL/MariaDB ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô + ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å PHP

‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á

-- ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á users
CREATE TABLE users (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    fullname VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á posts
CREATE TABLE posts (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    status ENUM('draft', 'published') DEFAULT 'draft',
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

-- ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á categories
CREATE TABLE categories (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    description TEXT
);

‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

  • INT - ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°
  • VARCHAR(n) - ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô n ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£
  • TEXT - ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å
  • DATE/DATETIME/TIMESTAMP - ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤
  • BOOLEAN/TINYINT(1) - ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á/‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏à
  • ENUM - ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î
  • AUTO_INCREMENT - ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  • PRIMARY KEY - ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥)
  • FOREIGN KEY - ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å (‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô)

‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (mysqli + prepared statements)

<?php
// config.php
$DB_HOST = "localhost";
$DB_USER = "dbuser";
$DB_PASS = "dbpass";
$DB_NAME = "schooldb";

// ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
$conn = mysqli_connect($DB_HOST, $DB_USER, $DB_PASS, $DB_NAME);

// ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠
if (!$conn) {
    die("‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ DB ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à: " . mysqli_connect_error());
}

// ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ charset
mysqli_set_charset($conn, "utf8");

    $fullname = trim($_POST["fullname"] ?? "");
    $email = trim($_POST["email"] ?? "");
    $password = $_POST["password"] ?? "";
    
    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
    if (empty($fullname) || empty($email) || empty($password)) {
        die("‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö");
    }
    
    // ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô
    $hashedPassword = password_hash($password, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
    
    // ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏° SQL statement
    $sql = "INSERT INTO users(fullname, email, password) VALUES(?, ?, ?)";
    $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
    
    if ($stmt) {
        // bind parameters
        mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "sss", $fullname, $email, $hashedPassword);
        
        // execute
        if (mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt)) {
            $newUserId = mysqli_insert_id($conn);
            echo "‡∏™‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à! ID: " . $newUserId;
        } else {
            echo "‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: " . mysqli_error($conn);
        }
        
        mysqli_stmt_close($stmt);
    } else {
        echo "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏° statement: " . mysqli_error($conn);

UPDATE: ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

<?php
require_once "config.php";

if ($_SERVER["REQUEST_METHOD"] == "POST") {
    $id = (int)$_POST["id"];
    $fullname = trim($_POST["fullname"]);
    $email = trim($_POST["email"]);
    
    if (empty($fullname) || empty($email) || $id <= 0) {
        die("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á");
    }

    $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
    mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "ssi", $fullname, $email, $id);
    
    if (mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt)) {
        echo "‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à";
    } else {
        echo "‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: " . mysqli_error($conn);
    }
}

    if (!$user) {
        die("‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ");
    }

?>

    <input type="hidden" name="id" value="<?= $user['id'] ?>">
    <input type="text" name="fullname" value="<?= htmlspecialchars($user['fullname']) ?>" required>

<?php
require_once "config.php";

    $id = (int)$_GET["id"];
    
    if ($id <= 0) {
        die("ID ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á");
    }
    
    $sql = "DELETE FROM users WHERE id=?";
    $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
    mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "i", $id);

        $affected = mysqli_stmt_affected_rows($stmt);
        if ($affected > 0) {
            echo "‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à";
        } else {
            echo "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö";
        }
    } else {
        echo "‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: " . mysqli_error($conn);
    }
} else if (isset($_GET["id"])) {
    $id = (int)$_GET["id"];
    echo "<p>‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà?</p>";
    echo "<a href='?id=$id&confirm=yes'>‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà, ‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢</a> | ";
    echo "<a href='users.php'>‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å</a>";

?>

<?php

    $sql .= " WHERE fullname LIKE ? OR email LIKE ?";
    $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
    $searchTerm = "%" . $search . "%";
    mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "ss", $searchTerm, $searchTerm);
    mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt);
    $result = mysqli_stmt_get_result($stmt);

    $result = mysqli_query($conn, $sql);
}

Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Prepared Statements ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ - ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô SQL Injection

  • ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Error - ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°

contact_save.php

<?php
require_once "config.php";

if ($_SERVER["REQUEST_METHOD"] == "POST") {
    $fullname = trim($_POST["fullname"] ?? "");
    $email = trim($_POST["email"] ?? "");
    $subject = trim($_POST["subject"] ?? "");
    $message = trim($_POST["message"] ?? "");
    
    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
    $errors = [];
    
    if (empty($fullname)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠-‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏∏‡∏•";
    }
    
    if (empty($email) || !filter_var($email, FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á";
    }
    
    if (empty($subject)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠";
    }
    
    if (empty($message)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°";
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ
        $createTable = "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contacts (
            id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
            fullname VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
            email VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
            subject VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
            message TEXT NOT NULL,
            created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        )";
        mysqli_query($conn, $createTable);
        
        // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
        $sql = "INSERT INTO contacts(fullname, email, subject, message) VALUES(?, ?, ?, ?)";
        $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
        mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "ssss", $fullname, $email, $subject, $message);
        
        if (mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt)) {
            echo "<div class='alert alert-success'>‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö</div>";
        } else {
            echo "<div class='alert alert-danger'>‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: " . mysqli_error($conn) . "</div>";
        }
    } else {
        foreach ($errors as $error) {
            echo "<div class='alert alert-danger'>$error</div>";
        }
    }
} else {
    header("Location: contact.php");
    exit;
}
?>

register_save.php

<?php
require_once "config.php";

if ($_SERVER["REQUEST_METHOD"] == "POST") {
    $course_id = (int)($_POST["course_id"] ?? 1);
    $firstname = trim($_POST["firstname"] ?? "");
    $lastname = trim($_POST["lastname"] ?? "");
    $email = trim($_POST["email"] ?? "");
    $phone = trim($_POST["phone"] ?? "");
    $company = trim($_POST["company"] ?? "");
    $dietary = trim($_POST["dietary"] ?? "");
    $agree = isset($_POST["agree"]);
    
    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
    $errors = [];
    
    if (empty($firstname)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠";
    }
    
    if (empty($lastname)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏∏‡∏•";
    }
    
    if (empty($email) || !filter_var($email, FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á";
    }
    
    if (empty($phone)) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå";
    }
    
    if (!$agree) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£";
    }
    
    // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥
    $checkEmail = "SELECT id FROM registrations WHERE email = ?";
    $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $checkEmail);
    mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "s", $email);
    mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt);
    $result = mysqli_stmt_get_result($stmt);
    
    if (mysqli_num_rows($result) > 0) {
        $errors[] = "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß";
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á
        $createTable = "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS registrations (
            id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
            course_id INT NOT NULL,
            firstname VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
            lastname VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
            email VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
            phone VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
            company VARCHAR(100),
            dietary TEXT,
            registration_number VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
            status ENUM('pending', 'confirmed', 'cancelled') DEFAULT 'pending',
            created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        )";
        mysqli_query($conn, $createTable);
        
        // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô
        $registration_number = 'REG' . date('Y') . sprintf('%04d', rand(1, 9999));
        
        // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
        $sql = "INSERT INTO registrations(course_id, firstname, lastname, email, phone, company, dietary, registration_number) 
                VALUES(?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)";
        $stmt = mysqli_prepare($conn, $sql);
        mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt, "isssssss", $course_id, $firstname, $lastname, $email, $phone, $company, $dietary, $registration_number);
        
        if (mysqli_stmt_execute($stmt)) {
            // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô
            header("Location: confirmation.php?reg=" . $registration_number);
            exit;
        } else {
            echo "<div class='alert alert-danger'>‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: " . mysqli_error($conn) . "</div>";
        }
    } else {
        include "includes/header.php";
        echo "<div class='container mt-5'>";
        foreach ($errors as $error) {
            echo "<div class='alert alert-danger'>$error</div>";
        }
        echo "<a href='javascript:history.back()' class='btn btn-primary'>‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç</a>";
        echo "</div>";
        include "includes/footer.php";
    }
} else {
    header("Location: courses.php");
    exit;
}

<?php

    header("Location: courses.php");
    exit;

// ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô
